msg:Big, clean rooms with full amenities. Curteous staff. Our room was in Building 2 and the lobby felt old in line with the look of the entire water town. The room, however, was modern, big, clean with full amenities.  The bed and pillow was even adjustable for the firmness. Could have also skipped this breakfast for the experience at the morning market. Very enjoyable stay at the hotel.  Only 1 thing,  it is not worth to pay for the balcony room on the top floor as it opens to a garden and not the river (no view). It may be better to take a normal room on the ground floor by the river. Also  have to take own luggage up the stair case if on top floor. Otherwise, excellent.

msg:I brought my baby to spend Children's Day on June 1st and chose a two-bedroom suite along the river at Tong'an Inn. The room is large, with beds and bathrooms on both floors, suitable for parent-child travel accommodation. It is very comfortable to stand by the window and watch the boats coming and going. The location is also good. The morning tea guest is just across the river, and the nearest pier and tour bus boarding point are also a few minutes' walk away.
I would like to praise the itinerary butler Xiao Yuan, who sent the parking lot location and some precautions one day in advance, and came to the parking lot to pick us up, helped with luggage and check-in, and sent messages and inquiries very late at night, and they were also very timely and patient.
Because it is along the river, there are still many mosquitoes, but the rooms are prepared with floral water, mosquito repellent, small electric fans, etc., which is quite thoughtful.

msg:Facilities: Although the booking website describes Building 1 as being built in 2015, it may be because it is arranged on the second floor, and it does not look old due to its ancient style. Everything a hotel should have is provided (plastic slippers are provided by yourself). (The buttons on the 233 TV remote control are very hard and insensitive. Change one. The black one on the embankment is quite useful)
Sanitation: Very clean, no odor at all in the room or the bathroom shower. Every day, you can see many cleaning staff busy on each floor. They are all cleaned up after the trip.
Environment: The first stop on the southern line of the scenic area, the hotel is a soy sauce garden attraction. It is a short walk from the water market with many activities. The dyeing workshop at Andufang Wharf is just around the corner. Other places can catch up with the station and take the tour bus. In fact, it is more comfortable to walk around with enough time. There are beautiful scenery everywhere in the hotel.
Service: You will receive a call from the hotel butler Xiaodang in the evening one day in advance‚òéÔ∏è, saving time to buy good things in advance, transport luggage, pick up and guide, explain the tour guide, in short, everything is covered. I knew about this pretty girl in advance (many hotel guests' comments), but I didn't expect to be lucky enough to meet her this time. The other staff of the hotel are very good. Many porters stand at the door when entering and leaving. It's quite a big scene. They are polite and smiling üòä and help a lot. The room card is invalid and can't open the door, which will be handled together. When checking out and changing hotels, a guy with glasses named Liao worked hard to carry the suitcase in and out, serving multiple guests, and helping to call a taxi.
Minibar first round: There are five kinds of drinks + 2 mineral waters.
The hotel breakfast is not bad, you can try it once. If you stay for two nights, you still have to experience the morning tea guest. You must make an appoin**ent when you check in, so as not to miss it.
This hotel restaurant 10% discount coupon: Linshui Restaurant signs the bill and notes the room number to get a 10% discount.
The scenic area is beautiful, with various activities and performances. You can experience the Jiangnan water town by slowing down and enjoying it.

In order to make it easier for us to take care of the elderly, the adjacent room was specially given to us, which is the best room in the entire building. Let‚Äôs talk about breakfast again. The dishes and fruits are fresh and the taste is suitable for north and south. The breakfast level is not as diverse as that of five-star hotels, and the quality is not inferior to that of five-star hotels. Finally, I would like to praise the housekeeper, Xiao Yuan, for his considerate service from the very beginning of check-in, and even more responsiveness to questions and requests during the entire check-in process. If there is a chance to come to Wuzhen again, I will definitely come again.
